My daughters couldn't believe I was listening to you... They asked me what I knew about you because I would play you all day...   But anyway, I heard to much pain along with amazing talent... It's your pain I heard that drew me to you and I just started praying for you but then I decided to pay more attention to your flow so I listened to your 1st album until when I 1st heard you and I did not skip one track... I have not listen to one rapper out here today like that but Wali 1st album and all of Kevin Gates music the same way... I'm cannot remember which one of yall I came across 1st but I do remember you two doing a song together... I discover both of you two came from the same city and area... So, I consider Kevin Gates and you as artists and not caught up with the industry BS politics... Living yall own life the way yall want to but I just want NBA Youngboy to know he is not alone out here... You are so young with a lot of life to live... I know it gets dark... There are real genuine ppl such as your fans on here and including me who genuinely cares for you and want you to stay strong... I promise you, life gets better... I wish I could coach you on a 1-on-1 about our mindset... They want us to destroy ourselves, it was designed that way...  You have so much healing to do, so much trauma in one young man's life and to feel like you are still alone even though there are ppl around you, that was once me and I'm here, successful, doing exactly what I want to do, my dream... All by changing my mindset, replacing all my negative thoughts with something positive... Instead of I can't or this is hard, or I have no one to love me, etc., replace those thoughts with I can and even though it's challenging, I got this and I'm going to start loving myself that way no one can hurt me... Believe in yourself, start with Self-Awareness, Self-Care, and Self-Love... We cannot give or receive love until we start loving ourselves 1st... We are who we attracts... So, if we won't genuine love from others, we have to start showing ourselves genuine love by starting with our mindset... How, when we get up in the morning and look in the mirror tell ourselves that we Love ourselves, say our name, feel it in our heart, mean it... Do this consistently everyday throughout the day if we find ourselves slipping into that dark space... I promise the more this is done, we will find ourselves in a much better mindset. We will find all the hurt and pain to start gradually going away...   Life will happen but we have the tools to get us through it... This is the beginning of using Emotional Intelligence... The more we use it, the better we get at it and living life becomes effortless even when we get trigger... It will not have the same affect...  NBA Youngboy, you can still drop those same bangers only this time when you are bringing that heat from the heart, you will not stay in that dark space... You now have the tools to bring yourself out of it... You will no longer feel that hurt and pain but you will still be able to express it all the same... This will not take away from your raw talent using your Emotional Intelligence... You are a natural gifted talented individual who are saving many lives rather you are aware or not... This is your purpose, this is your "Y" to save lives with your music...  Much Love, from an Ummi who cares deeply about your well being, you got this young King!!!
